## Diagram 2

```mermaid
flowchart TD
GET["GET /damageview/submission/:submissionId/fields"] --> Response["responseBody"]
Response --> Core["coreFields"]
Response --> Submission["submissionFields"]
Response --> Vin["vinFields"]
Response --> Images["imageFields"]
Submission --> LocationNode["location: dropdown (At Location, In Transit)"]
LocationNode -->|At Location| ReportingId["reportingLocationId: async dropdown (endpoint)"]
LocationNode -->|In Transit| ReportingInput["reportingLocation: input"]
Submission --> DamageNode["damageLocation: dropdown (In Yard/Bay, On Rail, Other)"]
DamageNode -->|In Yard/Bay| BayRelated["Bay fields: bayLocation, bayTag, frontRight, frontLeft, rearRight, rearLeft, overviewDamagedArea, closeupDamage, dashboardOverview, overviewWholeUnit"]
DamageNode -->|On Rail| RailRelated["Rail fields: railcarPosition, railcar, overviewDamagedArea, closeupDamage"]
DamageNode -->|Other| OtherRelated["Other fields: repairLocation"]
Submission --> OtherSubmission["other submissionFields: chockCondition, primaryChockType, railcarNumber, railcarType, secondarySubmitterEmail, secondarySubmitterPhoneNumber, unloadDate, additionalEmails, inProgressStatus, inProgressStatusUpdated, rejectedComments"]
Vin --> StolenVinNode["stolenVin: dropdown (notStolen, stolenMissing, stolenRecovered)"]
StolenVinNode -->|notStolen / stolenRecovered| AreaType["areaTypeSeverity: multiple_values → subFields(area, type, severity)"]
AreaType --> AreaNode["area: dropdown (codes 01..99)"]
AreaType --> TypeNode["type: dropdown (damage types)"]
AreaType --> SeverityNode["severity: dropdown (1..6)"]
Vin --> CommentsNode["comments: textarea (required)"]
Vin --> PositionNode["railcarPosition / bayLocation requiredWhen damageLocation == On Rail / In Yard/Bay"]
Images --> ImageRule["Images required when damageLocation ∈ {On Rail, In Yard/Bay} AND stolenVin ∈ {notStolen, stolenRecovered}"]
ImageRule --> BayTag["bayTag"]
ImageRule --> VINImage["vin"]
ImageRule --> FrontRight["frontRight"]
ImageRule --> FrontLeft["frontLeft"]
ImageRule --> RearRight["rearRight"]
ImageRule --> RearLeft["rearLeft"]
ImageRule --> OverviewDamagedArea["overviewDamagedArea"]
ImageRule --> CloseupDamage["closeupDamage"]
ImageRule --> RailcarImage["railcar"]
ImageRule --> DashboardOverview["dashboardOverview"]
ImageRule --> OverviewWholeUnit["overviewWholeUnit"]
ImageRule --> InteriorDamage["interiorDamage"]
ImageRule --> AdditionalPhoto["additionalPhoto"]
```

## Diagram 3

```mermaid
stateDiagram-v2
[*] --> FormIdle
FormIdle --> SelectLocation
SelectLocation --> LOC_AtLocation : At Location
SelectLocation --> LOC_InTransit : In Transit
LOC_AtLocation --> Show_ReportingLocationId
LOC_InTransit --> Show_ReportingLocation
FormIdle --> SelectDamage
SelectDamage --> DAM_InYardBay : In Yard/Bay
SelectDamage --> DAM_OnRail : On Rail
SelectDamage --> DAM_Other : Other
DAM_InYardBay --> ImagesConditionCheck
DAM_OnRail --> ImagesConditionCheck
DAM_Other --> NoImageRequirement
FormIdle --> SelectStolenVin
SelectStolenVin --> STOLEN_notStolen : notStolen
SelectStolenVin --> STOLEN_stolenMissing : stolenMissing
SelectStolenVin --> STOLEN_stolenRecovered : stolenRecovered
STOLEN_notStolen --> AreaTypeVisible
STOLEN_stolenRecovered --> AreaTypeVisible
STOLEN_stolenMissing --> AreaTypeHidden
ImagesConditionCheck --> ImagesRequired : stolenVin in {notStolen, stolenRecovered}
ImagesConditionCheck --> ImagesOptional : stolenVin == stolenMissing
ImagesRequired --> Show_ImageFields
AreaTypeVisible --> Show_AreaTypeSubFields
```
